File: C:\Users\laesc\OneDrive\Desktop\chester\evaluationbar.h
1: #ifndef EVALUATIONBAR_H
2: #define EVALUATIONBAR_H
3: 
4: #include <QPainter>
5: #include <QWidget>
6: 
7: // Update using syntax: bar->setEvaluation(-75.0);
8: 
9: class EvaluationBar : public QWidget
10: {
11:     Q_OBJECT
12: public:
13:     explicit EvaluationBar(QWidget *parent = nullptr) : QWidget(parent), evaluation(0.0) { }
14: 
15:     void setEvaluation(double eval) {
16:         evaluation = eval;
17:         update();  // Triggers a repaint
18:     }
19: 
20: protected:
21:     double scaleEvaluation(double eval) {
22:         const double scale = 100.0;  // Determines the scaling factor
23:         return scale * (std::log(std::abs(eval) + 1) / std::log(301));  // Log base change to scale from -300 to +300
24:     }
25: 
26:     void paintEvent(QPaintEvent *event) override {
27:         QPainter painter(this);
28:         painter.setRenderHint(QPainter::Antialiasing);
29:         painter.fillRect(rect(), Qt::white);
30: 
31:         // Adjust the evaluation using logarithmic scaling
32:         double adjustedEval = scaleEvaluation(evaluation);
33: 
34:         // Now map the adjusted evaluation to the bar width
35:         double blackPortion = (adjustedEval + 100.0) / 200.0;
36:         int blackWidth = static_cast<int>(width() * blackPortion);
37: 
38:         painter.fillRect(0, 0, blackWidth, height(), Qt::black);
39:     }
40: 
41: private:
42:     double evaluation;  // Store the evaluation from -100 to +100
43: };
44: 
45: #endif // EVALUATIONBAR_H

File: C:\Users\laesc\OneDrive\Desktop\chester\getfilecontents.py
1: import os
2: 
3: # Function to read file contents and write to output file
4: def read_files(directory, output_file):
5:     with open(output_file, 'a', encoding='utf-8') as out_file:
6:         for filename in os.listdir(directory):
7:             filepath = os.path.join(directory, filename)
8:             if os.path.isfile(filepath):
9:                 with open(filepath, 'r', encoding='utf-8', errors='ignore') as file:
10:                     out_file.write(f"File: {filepath}\n")
11:                     for i, line in enumerate(file, start=1):
12:                         out_file.write(f"{i}: {line}")
13:                     out_file.write("\n\n")
14: 
15: # Main function
16: def main():
17:     # Current directory
18:     current_dir = os.getcwd()
19:     output_file = "filecontents.txt"
20: 
21:     # Process files in the current directory
22:     read_files(current_dir, output_file)
23: 
24:     # Directories to process
25:     specified_directories = [
26:         "C:/Users/laesc/OneDrive/Desktop/chester/chess_classes",
27:         "C:/Users/laesc/OneDrive/Desktop/chester/chess_classes/piece_classes",
28:         "C:/Users/laesc/OneDrive/Desktop/chester/env",
29:         "C:/Users/laesc/OneDrive/Desktop/chester/ml",
30:         "C:/Users/laesc/OneDrive/Desktop/chester/python",
31:         "C:/Users/laesc/OneDrive/Desktop/chester/screens",
32:         "C:/Users/laesc/OneDrive/Desktop/chester/scripts",
33:         "C:/Users/laesc/OneDrive/Desktop/chester/styling"
34:         # Add more directories here if needed
35:     ]
36: 
37:     # Process specified directories
38:     for directory in specified_directories:
39:         if os.path.isdir(directory):
40:             read_files(directory, output_file)
41:         else:
42:             print(f"Directory '{directory}' not found.")
43: 
44: if __name__ == "__main__":
45:     main()

18: QString PythonInterface::getStats(QString UCI) {
19:     Py_Initialize();
20:     putenv("PYTHONWIN_HIDE_CONSOLE=1");
21:     SetEnvironmentVariableW(L"PYTHONWIN_HIDE_CONSOLE", L"1");
22: 
23:     QString result;
24:     std::string str_uci = UCI.toStdString();
25: 
26:     PyObject *pName = PyUnicode_FromString("get_stats");
27:     PyObject *pModule = PyImport_Import(pName);
28:     Py_DECREF(pName);
29:     // If the module is found
30:     if (pModule != NULL) {
31:         PyObject *pFunc = PyObject_GetAttrString(pModule, "get_game_stats");
32: 
33:         // If the function exists and is callable
34:         if (pFunc && PyCallable_Check(pFunc)) {
35:             PyObject* pArgs = PyTuple_Pack(1, PyUnicode_FromString(str_uci.c_str()));
36:             PyObject *pValue = PyObject_CallObject(pFunc, pArgs);
37:             Py_DECREF(pArgs);
38: 
39:             // If we recieve a return value
40:             if (pValue != NULL) {
41:                 QString return_value = PyUnicode_AsUTF8(pValue);
42:                 result = return_value;
43:                 Py_DECREF(pValue);
44:             } else {
45:                 // Else if the function didn't return anything
46:                 PyErr_Print();
47:                 fprintf(stderr, "Python function call failed\n");
48:             }
49:         } else {
50:             // Else if we cannot access the function
51:             PyErr_Print();
52:             fprintf(stderr, "Cannot find function get_board_evaluation\n");
53:         }
54:         Py_XDECREF(pFunc);
55:         Py_DECREF(pModule);
56:     } else {
57:         // Else if the module is not found
58:         PyErr_Print();
59:         fprintf(stderr, "Failed to load get_evaluation\n");
60:     }
61: 
62:     Py_Finalize();
63:     return result;
64: }
65:

115: QString PythonInterface::getNextMove(QString UCI)
116: {
117:     Py_Initialize();
118:     putenv("PYTHONWIN_HIDE_CONSOLE=1");

123: 
124:     PyObject *pName = PyUnicode_FromString("get_next_move");
125:     PyObject *pModule = PyImport_Import(pName);
126:     Py_DECREF(pName);
127:     // If the module is found
128:     if (pModule != NULL) {
129:         PyObject *pFunc = PyObject_GetAttrString(pModule, "get_next_best_move");
130: 
131:         // If the function exists and is callable
132:         if (pFunc && PyCallable_Check(pFunc)) {
133:             // PyObject* pArgs = PyUnicode_FromString(str_uci.c_str());
134:             PyObject* pArgs = PyTuple_Pack(1, PyUnicode_FromString(str_uci.c_str()));
135:             PyObject *pValue = PyObject_CallObject(pFunc, pArgs);
136:             Py_DECREF(pArgs);
137: 
138:             // If we recieve a return value
139:             if (pValue != NULL) {
140:                 QString return_value = PyUnicode_AsUTF8(pValue);
141:                 result = return_value;
142:                 Py_DECREF(pValue);
143:             } else {
144:                 // Else if the function didn't return anything
145:                 PyErr_Print();
146:                 fprintf(stderr, "Python function call failed\n");
147:             }
148:         } else {
149:             // Else if we cannot access the function

152:         }

File: C:\Users\laesc\OneDrive\Desktop\chester\README.md
1: [IN DEVELOPMENT]  
2:   
3: A chess game created using QtCreator written in C++, with a machine learning (neural networks) engine written in Python using PyTorch. 
4: 
5: See README.txt for details about project organization.


File: C:\Users\laesc\OneDrive\Desktop\chester\README.txt
1: directory organization:
2: 
3: 
4: |
5: |---chess_classes: contains C++ header and source files for the chess related objects
6: |   |
7: |   |---piece_classes: contains C++ header and source files for the six chess piece type classes
8: |
9: |---data: contains .pgn (portable game notation) files with chess game data for training the machine learning model
10: |
11: |---env: contains configuration class, environment variables in a JSON file, and steps to set up the development environment
12: |
13: |---icons: contains all of the icons used in the program and applicable attributions
14: |
15: |---logos: contains logos (should be combined into icons)
16: |
17: |---logs: contains steps in configuring development environment and worklog
18: |   |
19: |   |---color palettes: sample color palettes for reference in UX design
20: |
21: |---ml: contains all machine learning code
22: |
23: |---python: contains the python scripts used in the PythonInterface class
24: |
25: |---screens: contains all UI classes
26: |
27: |---scripts: contains all SQL scripts needed to create database (postgreSQL)
28: |
29: |---stockfish: contains the source code for the stockfish engine, which is currently being used as the engine for the game
30: |
31: |---styling: contains style class and Qt qss (css) file
32: |   |
33: |   |---color palettes: contains color palettes that may or may not be used for the design of the game
34: |   |
35: |   |---fonts: contains fonts used by qss file

12: #include "pythoninterface.h"

17: #include <QElapsedTimer>

19: /* Constructor */
20: ChessBoard::ChessBoard(QWidget* parent) : QWidget(parent) {
21:     chessScene = new QGraphicsScene(this);
22:     chessScene->setBackgroundBrush(Qt::transparent);
23: 
24:     chessView = new QGraphicsView(chessScene, this);
25:     chessView->setBackgroundBrush(Qt::transparent);
26:     chessView->setFrameStyle(QFrame::NoFrame);
27:     chessView->setFixedSize(700, 700);
28:     chessView->setSizePolicy(QSizePolicy::Expanding, QSizePolicy::Expanding);
29:     chessView->fitInView(chessScene->sceneRect(), Qt::KeepAspectRatio);
30: 
31:     QVBoxLayout* layout = new QVBoxLayout(this);
32:     layout->addWidget(chessView);
33:     setLayout(layout);
34:     this->config = new Config();
35:     config->refreshConfig();
36: 
37:     createChessBoard();
38:     loadStartingPosition();
39: }
40: 
41: void ChessBoard::start_time()
42: {
43:     start = clock();
44:     return;
45: }
46: 
47: void ChessBoard::end_time(QString name)
48: {
49:     end = clock();
50:     qDebug() << name << "ran for" << double(end - start) / CLOCKS_PER_SEC;
51:     return;
52: }
53: 
54: // ---------------------------------------- //
55: // CHESS BOARD RELATED FUNCTIONS //
56: // ---------------------------------------- //
57: 
58: // The 64 chess board ChessSquare objects created here
59: void ChessBoard::createChessBoard() {
60:     //    qDebug() << "====== Entering createChessBoard";
61:     for (int rank = 0; rank < 8; rank++) {
62:         for (int file = 0; file < 8; file++) {
63:             ChessSquare *square = new ChessSquare(file * tileSize, rank * tileSize, tileSize, tileSize, this->config->getColor());
64:             square->setPen(Qt::NoPen);
65:             chessScene->addItem(square);
66: 
67:             // Set each entry in the array to a ChessSquare
68:             boardSquares[rank][file] = square;
69:             square->setRank(rank);
70:             square->setFile(file);
71: 
72:             connect(square, &ChessSquare::squareLeftClicked, this, &ChessBoard::squareLeftClicked);
73:             connect(square, &ChessSquare::squareRightClicked, this, &ChessBoard::squareRightClicked);
74:         }
75:     }
76: }
77: 
78: // Creates all the ChessPiece objects
79: void ChessBoard::loadStartingPosition() {
80:     // Pawns
81:     for (int i = 0; i < 2; i ++) {
82:         for (int j = 0; j < 8; j++) {
83:             int rank = (i == 0) ? 1 : 6;
84: 
85:             Pawn *pawn = new Pawn(this->config->getColor());
86: 
87:             if (rank == 6) {
88:                 if (config->getColor() == true) {
89:                     pawn->setWhite(true);
90:                 } else {
91:                     pawn->setWhite(false);
92:                 }
93:             } else {
94:                 if (config->getColor() == true) {
95:                     pawn->setWhite(false);
96:                 } else {
97:                     pawn->setWhite(true);
98:                 }
99:             }
100: 
101:             int color = pawn->getWhite() == true ? 1 : 2;
102:             addPieceToSquare(pawn, rank, j, color);
103:         }
104:     }
105: 
106:     // Rooks
107:     int rookFlag = 0;
108:     for (int i = 0; i < 2; i ++) {
109:         for (int j = 0; j < 2; j++) {
110:             int rank = (i == 0) ? 0 : 7;
111:             int file = (j == 0) ? 0 : 7;
112: 
113:             Rook *rook = new Rook(this->config->getColor());
114: 
115:             if (rank == 7) {
116:                 // Rank 7, white pieces
117:                 if (config->getColor() == true) {
118:                     rook->setWhite(true);
119:                 } else {
120:                     rook->setWhite(false);
121:                 }
122:                 if (file == 0) {
123:                     // File 0, kingside
124:                     whiteKingsideRook = rook;
125:                 } else {
126:                     // File 7, queenside
127:                     whiteQueensideRook = rook;
128:                 }
129:             } else {
130:                 // Rank 0, black pieces
131:                 if (config->getColor() == true) {
132:                     rook->setWhite(false);
133:                 } else {
134:                     rook->setWhite(true);
135:                 }
136:                 if (file == 0) {
137:                     // File 0, kingside
138:                     blackKingsideRook = rook;
139:                 } else {
140:                     // File 7, queenside
141:                     blackQueensideRook = rook;
142:                 }
143:             }
144: 
145:             int color = rook->getWhite() == true ? 1 : 2;
146:             addPieceToSquare(rook, rank, file, color);
147:             rookFlag ++;
148:         }
149:     }
150: 
151:     //  Knights
152:     for (int i = 0; i < 2; i ++) {
153:         for (int j = 0; j < 2; j++) {
154:             int rank = (i == 0) ? 0 : 7;
155:             int file = (j == 0) ? 1 : 6;
156: 
157:             Knight *knight = new Knight(this->config->getColor());
158: 
159:             if (rank == 7) {
160:                 if (config->getColor() == true) {
161:                     knight->setWhite(true);
162:                 } else {
163:                     knight->setWhite(false);
164:                 }
165:             } else {
166:                 if (config->getColor() == true) {
167:                     knight->setWhite(false);
168:                 } else {
169:                     knight->setWhite(true);
170:                 }
171:             }
172: 
173:             int color = knight->getWhite() == true ? 1 : 2;
174:             addPieceToSquare(knight, rank, file, color);
175:         }
176:     }
177: 
178:     // Bishops
179:     for (int i = 0; i < 2; i ++) {
180:         for (int j = 0; j < 2; j++) {
181:             int rank = (i == 0) ? 0 : 7;
182:             int file = (j == 0) ? 2 : 5;
183: 
184:             Bishop *bishop = new Bishop(this->config->getColor());
185: 
186:             if (rank == 7) {
187:                 if (config->getColor() == true) {
188:                     bishop->setWhite(true);
189:                 } else {
190:                     bishop->setWhite(false);
191:                 }
192:             } else {
193:                 if (config->getColor() == true) {
194:                     bishop->setWhite(false);
195:                 } else {
196:                     bishop->setWhite(true);
197:                 }
198:             }
199: 
200:             int color = bishop->getWhite() == true ? 1 : 2;
201:             addPieceToSquare(bishop, rank, file, color);
202:         }
203:     }
204: 
205:     // Kings
206:     for (int i = 0; i < 2; i ++) {
207:         for (int j = 0; j < 1; j++) {
208:             int rank = (i == 0) ? 0 : 7;
209:             int file = (j == 0) ? 4 : 4;
210: 
211:             King *king = new King(this->config->getColor());
212: 
213:             if (rank == 7) {
214:                 if (config->getColor() == true) {
215:                     whiteKing = king;
216:                     king->setWhite(true);
217:                 } else {
218:                     blackKing = king;
219:                     king->setWhite(false);
220:                 }
221:             } else {
222:                 if (config->getColor() == true) {
223:                     blackKing = king;
224:                     king->setWhite(false);
225:                 } else {
226:                     whiteKing = king;
227:                     king->setWhite(true);
228:                 }
229:             }
230: 
231:             king->rank = rank;
232:             king->file = file;
233: 
234:             int color = king->getWhite() == true ? 1 : 2;
235:             addPieceToSquare(king, rank, file, color);
236:         }
237:     }
238: 
239:     // Queens
240:     for (int i = 0; i < 2; i ++) {
241:         for (int j = 0; j < 1; j++) {
242:             int rank = (i == 0) ? 0 : 7;
243:             int file = (j == 0) ? 3 : 3;
244: 
245:             Queen *queen = new Queen(this->config->getColor());
246: 
247:             if (rank == 7) {
248:                 if (config->getColor() == true) {
249:                     queen->setWhite(true);
250:                 } else {
251:                     queen->setWhite(false);
252:                 }
253:             } else {
254:                 if (config->getColor() == true) {
255:                     queen->setWhite(false);
256:                 } else {
257:                     queen->setWhite(true);
258:                 }
259:             }
260: 
261:             int color = queen->getWhite() == true ? 1 : 2;
262:             addPieceToSquare(queen, rank, file, color);
263:         }
264:     }
265: }
266: 
267: // Connect  to python engine and get the next best move
268: void ChessBoard::getNextMove(std::string nextMove)
269: {
270:     nextBestMoveSquares.clear();
271: 
272:     std::string startFile, endFile, startRank, endRank;
273: 
274:     startFile = nextMove.substr(0, 1);
275:     startRank = nextMove.substr(1, 1);
276:     endFile = nextMove.substr(2, 1);
277:     endRank = nextMove.substr(3, 1);
278: 
279:     int startRankInt = abs((startRank[0] - 48) - 8);
280:     int endRankInt = abs((endRank[0] - 48) - 8);
281:     int startFileInt = startFile[0] - 97;
282:     int endFileInt = endFile[0] - 97;
283: 
284:     ChessSquare *startSquare = this->getSquare(startRankInt, startFileInt);
285:     ChessSquare *endSquare = this->getSquare(endRankInt, endFileInt);
286: 
287:     nextBestMoveSquares.push_back(endSquare);
288:     nextBestMoveSquares.push_back(startSquare);
289: 
290:     return;
291: }
292: 
293: // Connect to python engine and get current evaluation
294: void ChessBoard::getEvaluation(std::string game_eval) {
295:     // Process the evaluation
296:     int separator = game_eval.find('?');
297: 
298:     // Get the game state
299:     eval.status = (game_eval.substr(separator + 1) == "cp") ? 1 : 2;
300: 
301:     // Get the evaluation value
302:     std::stringstream(game_eval.substr(0, separator)) >> eval.value;
303: 
304:     // Determine who is winning
305:     eval.winning = eval.value >= 0 ? 1 : 2;
306: 
307:     // After determining who is winning, now can take abs value of value
308:     eval.value = std::abs(eval.value);
309:     return;
310: }
311: 
312: void ChessBoard::getStats()
313: {
314:     PythonInterface *python = new PythonInterface();
315:     QString UCI = this->boardToUCI();
316:     std::string result = python->getStats(UCI).toStdString();
317: 
318:     // Separate the results
319:     int separator = result.find('&');
320:     std::string nextMove = result.substr(0, separator);
321:     getNextMove(nextMove);
322: 
323:     std::string game_eval = result.substr(separator+1);
324:     getEvaluation(game_eval);
325:     qDebug() << "MOVE:" << nextMove;
326:     qDebug() << "GAME EVAL:" << game_eval;
327: 
328:     return;
329: }
330: 
331: std::vector<ChessSquare *> ChessBoard::getPossibleMoves(ChessSquare *square)
332: {
333:     ChessPiece *selectedPiece = square->getOccupyingPiece();
334: 
335:     std::vector<ChessSquare*> moves;
336:     std::vector<int> coords = selectedPiece->getMovesVector();
337:     bool lineStopped = false; // Marked true when ecountering a square with friendly piece, since you cannot move through them
338: 
339:     // Highlight potential moves yellow
340:     for (int i = 0; i < (int) coords.size(); i+=2)
341:     {
342:         int newRank, newFile;
343: 
344:         // Pull set of coordinates from vector
345:         int x = coords[i];
346:         int y = coords[i+1];
347: 
348:         // Reset lineStopped when a new direction is started (marked by 0, 0 coords)
349:         if (x == 0 && y == 0) {
350:             lineStopped = false;
351:             continue;
352:         }
353: 
354:         if (lineStopped == false) {
355:             if (selectedPiece->getWhite() != true) {
356:                 // Close side of board
357:                 newFile = square->getFile() - x;          // Change in x-axis
358:                 newRank = square->getRank() + y;     // Change in y-axis
359:             } else {
360:                 // Far side of board
361:                 newFile = square->getFile() + x;          // Change in x-axis
362:                 newRank = square->getRank() - y;     // Change in y-axis
363:             }
364: 
365:             // Only move forward if coordinate is on the board
366:             if (newRank < 8 && newFile < 8 && newRank >= 0 && newFile >= 0) {
367:                 ChessSquare *possibleMove = this->getSquare(newRank, newFile);
368:                 bool possibleMoveOccupied = possibleMove->getOccupyingPiece() == nullptr ? false : true;
369: 
370:                 if (possibleMoveOccupied == false) {
371:                     // If square is not occupied, it is a potential move
372:                     moves.push_back(possibleMove);
373:                 } else if (selectedPiece->getWhite() == true && possibleMove->getOccupyingPiece()->getWhite() == false) {
374:                     // If selected piece is white and target piece is black, it is potential move but blocks the line
375:                     moves.push_back(possibleMove);
376:                     lineStopped = true;
377:                 } else if (selectedPiece->getWhite() == false && possibleMove->getOccupyingPiece()->getWhite() == true) {
378:                     // If selected piece is black and target piece is white, it is potential move but blocks the line
379:                     possibleMoveSquares.push_back(possibleMove);
380:                     lineStopped = true;
381:                 } else {
382:                     // If square is occupied by friendly, that is blocks the line
383:                     lineStopped = true;
384:                 }
385:             }
386:         }
387:     }
388: 
389:     if (selectedPiece->getName() == "Pawn") {
390:         // Check attack squares for pawns
391:         std::vector<int> attackCoords = { -1, 1, 1, 1 };
392: 
393:         // Highlight potential moves yellow
394:         for (int i = 0; i < (int) attackCoords.size(); i+=2)
395:         {
396:             int newRank, newFile;
397: 
398:             // Pull set of coordinates from vector
399:             int x = coords[i];
400:             int y = coords[i+1];
401: 
402:             if (selectedPiece->getWhite() != true) {
403:                 // Close side of board
404:                 newFile = square->getFile() - x;          // Change in x-axis
405:                 newRank = square->getRank() + y;     // Change in y-axis
406:             } else {
407:                 // Far side of board
408:                 newFile = square->getFile() + x;          // Change in x-axis
409:                 newRank = square->getRank() - y;     // Change in y-axis
410:             }
411: 
412:             // Only move forward if coordinate is on the board
413:             if (newRank < 8 && newFile < 8 && newRank >= 0 && newFile >= 0) {
414:                 ChessSquare *possibleMove = this->getSquare(newRank, newFile);
415:                 bool possibleMoveOccupied = possibleMove->getOccupyingPiece() == nullptr ? false : true;
416:                 if (possibleMoveOccupied == true) {
417:                     possibleMoveSquares.push_back(possibleMove);
418:                 }
419:             }
420:         }
421:     }
422: 
423:     return moves;
424: }
425: 
426: // TODO place this somewhere and pass the kings rank, file, color, if its coming from check already to it
427: bool ChessBoard::checkCheck(int kingRank, int kingFile, bool isWhite, bool check) {
428: 
429:     std:: vector<int> directionsVector = {
430:         1, -1,
431:         2, -2,
432:         3, -3,
433:         4, -4,
434:         5, -5,
435:         6, -6,
436:         7, -7,
437:         0, 0,
438:         1, 1,
439:         2, 2,
440:         3, 3,
441:         4, 4,
442:         5, 5,
443:         6, 6,
444:         7, 7,
445:         0, 0,
446:         -1, 1,
447:         -2, 2,
448:         -3, 3,
449:         -4, 4,
450:         -5, 5,
451:         -6, 6,
452:         -7, 7,
453:         0, 0,
454:         -1, -1,
455:         -2, -2,
456:         -3, -3,
457:         -4, -4,
458:         -5, -5,
459:         -6, -6,
460:         -7, -7,
461:         0, 0,
462:         0, -1,
463:         0, -2,
464:         0, -3,
465:         0, -4,
466:         0, -5,
467:         0, -6,
468:         0, -7,
469:         0, 0,
470:         0, 1,
471:         0, 2,
472:         0, 3,
473:         0, 4,
474:         0, 5,
475:         0, 6,
476:         0, 7,
477:         0, 0,
478:         1, 0,
479:         2, 0,
480:         3, 0,
481:         4, 0,
482:         5, 0,
483:         6, 0,
484:         7, 0,
485:         0, 0,
486:         -1, 0,
487:         -2, 0,
488:         -3, 0,
489:         -4, 0,
490:         -5, 0,
491:         -6, 0,
492:         -7, 0,
493:     };
494: 
495:     bool lineStopped = false;
496:     int newRank, newFile;
497: 
498:     ChessSquare *kingSquare = boardSquares[kingRank][kingFile];
499: 
500:     // For each coordinate
501:     for (int i = 0; i < (int) directionsVector.size(); i+=2) {
502: 
503:         // Pull set of coordinates from vector
504:         int x = directionsVector[i];
505:         int y = directionsVector[i+1];
506: 
507:         // Reset lineStopped when a new direction is started (marked by 0, 0 coords)
508:         if (x == 0 && y == 0) {
509:             lineStopped = false;
510:             continue;
511:         }
512: 
513:         // Determine the next square to check
514:         if (lineStopped == false) {
515:             if (isWhite != true) {
516:                 // Light pieces
517:                 newFile = kingSquare->getFile() - x;          // Change in x-axis
518:                 newRank = kingSquare->getRank() + y;     // Change in y-axis
519:             } else {
520:                 // Dark pieces
521:                 newFile = kingSquare->getFile() + x;          // Change in x-axis
522:                 newRank = kingSquare->getRank() - y;     // Change in y-axis
523:             }
524: 
525:             // Only move forward if coordinate is on the board
526:             if (newRank < 8 && newFile < 8 && newRank >= 0 && newFile >= 0) {
527:                 ChessSquare *squareToCheck = this->getSquare(newRank, newFile);
528:                 bool squareOccupied = squareToCheck->getOccupyingPiece() == nullptr ? false : true;
529: 
530:                 // Only move forward if the square is occupied
531:                 if (squareOccupied == false) {
532:                     // Do nothing
533:                 } else {
534:                     ChessPiece *piece = squareToCheck->getOccupyingPiece();
535: 
536:                     if (piece->getWhite() == isWhite) {
537:                         // If square is occupied by friendly, that is blocks the line
538:                         lineStopped = true;
539:                     } else {
540:                         std::vector<ChessSquare*> moves = getPossibleMoves(squareToCheck);
541: 
542:                         // If the kings square is in the pieces possible moves, then check is present
543:                         for (ChessSquare* testingSquare : moves) {
544:                             if (kingSquare == testingSquare) {
545:                                 // CHECK
546:                                 // Check for any escape
547:                                 if (check == false) {
548:                                     QColor color = QColor(188, 143, 143);
549:                                     if (config->getAssistModeOn() == true) { kingSquare->toggleSquareCustom(color); }
550:                                     bool endgame = checkmateCheck(kingSquare, isWhite);
551:                                     if (endgame == true) {
552:                                         endGame(kingSquare);
553:                                     }
554:                                 }
555:                                 return true;
556:                             }
557:                         }
558:                     }
559:                 }
560:             }
561:         }
562:     }
563:     return false;
564: }
565: 
566: bool ChessBoard::checkmateCheck(ChessSquare *kingSquare, bool isWhite)
567: {
568:     // Get the possible moves that the king has
569:     std::vector<ChessSquare*> kingsMoves = getPossibleMoves(kingSquare);
570:     bool danger = true;
571: 
572:     // If no moves then mate
573:     if (kingsMoves.empty() == true) {
574:         endGame(kingSquare);
575:     } else {
576:         // Check to see if any possible squares are safe
577:         for (ChessSquare* testingSquare : kingsMoves) {
578:             bool danger = checkCheck(testingSquare->getRank(), testingSquare->getFile(), isWhite, true);
579:             if (danger == false) {
580:                 QColor color = QColor(176,196,222);
581:                 if (config->getAssistModeOn() == true) { testingSquare->toggleSquareCustom(color); }
582:                 return false;
583:             }
584:         }
585:     }
586:     return danger;
587: }
588: 
589: void ChessBoard::endGame(ChessSquare *square)
590: {
591:     ChessPiece *loser = square->getOccupyingPiece();
592:     QString color = loser->getWhite() == true ? "White" : "Black";
593:     QString notification = "Game Over! " + color + " loses!";
594: 
595:     // Disable all chess squares
596:     for (int rank = 0; rank < 8; rank++) {
597:         for (int file = 0; file < 8; file++) {
598:             ChessSquare *square = boardSquares[rank][file];
599:             square->setDisabled(true);
600:         }
601:     }
602: 
603:     Q_EMIT game_over(notification);
604: 
605:     return;
606: }

622: // Returns true if the specified chess quare object is a valid place to move
623: bool ChessBoard::squareInPossibleMoves(ChessSquare *square)
624: {
625:     for (ChessSquare *s : possibleMoveSquares) {
626:         if (s == square) {
627:             return true;
628:         }
629:     }
630:     return false;
631: }
632: 
633: // Reset all yellow squares to original color
634: void ChessBoard::resetHighlightedSquares() {
635:     while (!highlightedSquares.empty()) {
636:         ChessSquare *square = highlightedSquares.back();
637:         highlightedSquares.pop_back();
638:         square->resetColor();
639:     }
640:     return;
641: }
642: 
643: // Reset all red squares to original color
644: void ChessBoard::resetRedSquares() {
645:     while (!redSquares.empty()) {
646:         ChessSquare *square = redSquares.back();
647:         redSquares.pop_back();
648:         square->resetColor();
649:     }
650:     return;
651: }
652: 
653: // Empty the possible moves vector
654: void ChessBoard::resetPossibleMoveSquares() {
655:     while(!possibleMoveSquares.empty()) {
656:         possibleMoveSquares.pop_back();
657:     }
658:     return;
659: }

661: void ChessBoard::printMoveDebug(QString header) {
662:     qDebug() << header;
663:     if (selectedSquare != nullptr) { qDebug() << "Selected square:" << selectedSquare->getRank() << selectedSquare->getFile(); } else { qDebug() << "No selected square"; }
664:     if (!highlightedSquares.empty()) { qDebug() << "Highlighted squares is NOT empty."; } else { qDebug() << "Highlighted squares is empty."; }
665:     if (!possibleMoveSquares.empty()) { qDebug() << "Possible moves is NOT empty"; } else { qDebug() << "Possible moves is empty"; }
666:     qDebug() << Qt::endl;
667: 
668:     return;
669: }

674: 
675: // Runs only if square clicked has piece on it! Highlight all potential moves based on the piece selected
676: void ChessBoard::highlightPossibleSquares(ChessSquare *square) {
677:     ChessPiece *selectedPiece = square->getOccupyingPiece();
678:     selectPiece(selectedPiece, square);
679: 
680:     std::vector<int> coords = selectedPiece->getMovesVector();
681:     bool lineStopped = false; // Marked true when ecountering a square with friendly piece, since you cannot move through them
682: 
683:     // Highlight potential moves yellow
684:     for (int i = 0; i < (int) coords.size(); i+=2)
685:     {
686:         int newRank, newFile;
687: 
688:         // Pull set of coordinates from vector
689:         int x = coords[i];
690:         int y = coords[i+1];
691: 
692:         // Reset lineStopped when a new direction is started (marked by 0, 0 coords)
693:         if (x == 0 && y == 0) {
694:             lineStopped = false;
695:             continue;
696:         }
697: 
698:         if (lineStopped == false) {
699:             if (selectedPiece->getWhite() != true) {
700:                 if (config->getColor() == true) {
701:                     // Opp side
702:                     newFile = square->getFile() - x;          // Change in x-axis
703:                     newRank = square->getRank() + y;     // Change in y-axis
704:                 } else {
705:                     newFile = square->getFile() + x;          // Change in x-axis
706:                     newRank = square->getRank() - y;     // Change in y-axis
707:                 }
708:             } else {
709:                 // Player side
710:                 if (config->getColor() == true) {
711:                     newFile = square->getFile() + x;          // Change in x-axis
712:                     newRank = square->getRank() - y;     // Change in y-axis
713:                 } else {
714:                     newFile = square->getFile() - x;          // Change in x-axis
715:                     newRank = square->getRank() + y;     // Change in y-axis
716:                 }
717:             }
718: 
719:             // Only move forward if coordinate is on the board
720:             if (newRank < 8 && newFile < 8 && newRank >= 0 && newFile >= 0) {
721:                 ChessSquare *possibleMove = this->getSquare(newRank, newFile);
722:                 bool squareOccupied = possibleMove->getOccupyingPiece() == nullptr ? false : true;
723:                 // if (squareOccupied == true) { qDebug()<< "Square occupied by:" << possibleMove->getOccupyingPiece()->getName(); }
724: 
725:                 if (squareOccupied == false) {
726:                     // If square is not occupied, it is a potential move
727:                     if (config->getAssistModeOn() == true) { possibleMove->toggleSquareYellow(); }
728:                     highlightedSquares.push_back(possibleMove);
729:                     possibleMoveSquares.push_back(possibleMove);
730:                     movePending = true;
731:                 } else if (selectedPiece->getWhite() == true && possibleMove->getOccupyingPiece()->getWhite() == false) {
732:                     // If selected piece is white and target piece is black, it is potential move but blocks the line
733:                     if (selectedPiece->getName() != "Pawn") {
734:                         if (config->getAssistModeOn() == true) { possibleMove->toggleSquareYellow(); }
735:                         highlightedSquares.push_back(possibleMove);
736:                         possibleMoveSquares.push_back(possibleMove);
737:                         movePending = true;
738:                         lineStopped = true;
739:                     }
740:                 } else if (selectedPiece->getWhite() == false && possibleMove->getOccupyingPiece()->getWhite() == true) {
741:                     // If selected piece is black and target piece is white, it is potential move but blocks the line
742:                     if (selectedPiece->getName() != "Pawn") {
743:                         if (config->getAssistModeOn() == true) { possibleMove->toggleSquareYellow(); }
744:                         highlightedSquares.push_back(possibleMove);
745:                         possibleMoveSquares.push_back(possibleMove);
746:                         movePending = true;
747:                         lineStopped = true;
748:                     }
749:                 } else {
750:                     // If square is occupied by friendly, that is blocks the line
751:                     lineStopped = true;
752:                 }
753:             }
754:         }
755:     }
756: 
757:     if (selectedPiece->getName() == "Pawn") {
758:         // Check attack squares for pawns
759:         std::vector<int> attackCoords = { -1, 1, 1, 1 };
760: 
761:         // Highlight potential moves yellow
762:         for (int i = 0; i < (int) attackCoords.size(); i+=2)
763:         {
764:             int attackRank, attackFile;
765: 
766:             // Pull set of coordinates from vector
767:             int attackx = attackCoords[i];
768:             int attacky = attackCoords[i+1];
769: 
770:             if (selectedPiece->getWhite() != true) {
771:                 if (config->getColor() == true) {
772:                     // Opp side
773:                     attackRank = square->getFile() - attackx;          // Change in x-axis
774:                     attackFile = square->getRank() + attacky;     // Change in y-axis
775:                 } else {
776:                     attackFile = square->getFile() + attackx;          // Change in x-axis
777:                     attackRank = square->getRank() - attacky;     // Change in y-axis
778:                 }
779:             } else {
780:                 // Player side
781:                 if (config->getColor() == true) {
782:                     attackFile = square->getFile() + attackx;          // Change in x-axis
783:                     attackRank = square->getRank() - attacky;     // Change in y-axis
784:                 } else {
785:                     attackFile = square->getFile() - attackx;          // Change in x-axis
786:                     attackRank = square->getRank() + attacky;     // Change in y-axis
787:                 }
788:             }
789: 
790:             // Only move forward if coordinate is on the board
791:             if (attackRank < 8 && attackFile < 8 && attackRank >= 0 && attackFile >= 0) {
792:                 ChessSquare *attackMove = this->getSquare(attackRank, attackFile);
793:                 bool possibleMoveOccupied = attackMove->getOccupyingPiece() == nullptr ? false : true;
794:                 if (possibleMoveOccupied == true) {
795:                     if (config->getAssistModeOn() == true) { attackMove->toggleSquareYellow(); }
796:                     possibleMoveSquares.push_back(attackMove);
797:                     highlightedSquares.push_back(attackMove);
798:                 }
799:             }
800:         }
801:     }
802:     return;
803: }
804: 
805: // This slot runs if the user left clicks on a square
806: void ChessBoard::squareLeftClicked(int rank, int file)
807: {
808:     checkCheck(whiteKing->rank, whiteKing->file, true, false);
809:     checkCheck(blackKing->rank, blackKing->file, false, false);
810: 
811:     // Check that click was legal
812:     if (boardSquares[rank][file] == nullptr) {
813:         qDebug() << "User has somehow clicked on a square that does not exist";
814:     } else {
815:         ChessSquare *squareClicked = this->getSquare(rank, file);
816: 
817:         // If move currently pending
818:         if (movePending == true) {
819:             if (squareInPossibleMoves(squareClicked) == true) {
820:                 movePiece(squareClicked); // Move piece will deselect piece, empty out highlight and move vectors, reset base square color
821:                 // getStats(); // TODO
822:                 Q_EMIT moveCompleted(lastMove, eval.winning, eval.value);
823:                 // moveBlack();
824:                 checkCheck(whiteKing->rank, whiteKing->file, true, false);
825:                 checkCheck(blackKing->rank, blackKing->file, false, false);
826:             } else {
827:                 movePending = false;
828:                 deselectPiece(selectedSquare->getOccupyingPiece(), selectedSquare);
829:                 resetPossibleMoveSquares();
830:                 resetHighlightedSquares();
831: 
832:                 // If the square is not already selected
833:                 if (selectedSquare != squareClicked) {
834:                     selectSquare(squareClicked);
835:                 } else { // Else if the square was already actively selected (deselect square)
836:                     deselectSquare(squareClicked);
837:                 }
838:             }
839:         } else {
840:             // Reset data from previous click
841:             resetPossibleMoveSquares();
842:             resetHighlightedSquares();
843: 
844:             if (selectedSquare != nullptr) {
845:                 // If the square is not already selected
846:                 if (selectedSquare != squareClicked) {
847:                     if (selectedSquare->getOccupyingPiece() != nullptr) {
848:                         deselectPiece(selectedSquare->getOccupyingPiece(), selectedSquare);
849:                     }
850:                     selectSquare(squareClicked);
851:                 } else { // Else if the square was already actively selected (deselect square)
852:                     deselectSquare(squareClicked);
853:                     if (squareClicked->getOccupyingPiece() != nullptr) {
854:                         deselectPiece(squareClicked->getOccupyingPiece(), squareClicked);
855:                     }
856:                 }
857:             } else {
858:                 selectSquare(squareClicked);
859:             }
860:         }
861:     }
862: 
863:     qDebug() << "----------------------------------------------------------------";
864:     return;
865: }

867: // This slot runs if the user right clicks on a square, it:
868: //   - highlights the square red
869: //   - adds the squars to redSquares vector
870: void ChessBoard::squareRightClicked(int rank, int file) {
871:     ChessSquare *square = boardSquares[rank][file];
872:     QColor color = QColor(164,90,82);
873:     square->toggleSquareCustom(color);
874:     redSquares.push_back(square);
875:     return;
876: }

878: void ChessBoard::selectSquare(ChessSquare *squareClicked) {
879:     if (selectedSquare != nullptr) {
880:         selectedSquare->resetColor();
881:     }
882:     selectedSquare = squareClicked;
883:     squareClicked->toggleSquareYellow();
884:     if (squareClicked->getOccupyingPiece() != nullptr) {
885:         ChessPiece *piece = squareClicked->getOccupyingPiece();
886:         bool white = piece->getWhite();
887:         if (white == true && whiteToPlay == true) {
888:             highlightPossibleSquares(squareClicked);
889:         } else if (white == true && whiteToPlay == false) {
890: 
891:         } else if (white == false && whiteToPlay == false) {
892:             highlightPossibleSquares(squareClicked);
893:         } else {
894: 
895:         }
896:     }
897: 
898:     return;
899: }
900: 
901: void ChessBoard::deselectSquare(ChessSquare * squareClicked) {
902:     if (squareClicked != nullptr) {
903:         squareClicked->resetColor();
904:     }
905:     selectedSquare = nullptr;
906: 
907:     return;
908: }
909: 
910: // -------------------------------------- //
911: // CHESS PIECE RELATED FUNCTIONS //
912: // -------------------------------------- //
913: 
914: // This function is the driver funtion for moving pieces, and is responsible to:
915: // - move the piece sprite
916: // - deselect piece
917: // - empty out highlighted square vector
918: // - empty out possible move vector
919: // - reset selectedsquare color
920: // - set selectedsquare to nullptr
921: // - set movepending to false
922: // - toggle pawn moved flag
923: // - toggle rook moved flag
924: // - toggle king moved flag
925: // - update half move counter
926: // - update full move counter
927: // - save lastmove in algebraic notation
928: // - update what color is to play
929: // - update lastmovedpiece
930: // - check for en passant status
931: //
932: void ChessBoard::movePiece(ChessSquare *squareClicked)
933: {
934:     ChessPiece *pieceToMove = selectedSquare->getOccupyingPiece(); // Get piece from old square
935:     lastMove = moveToAlgebraic(pieceToMove, squareClicked);
936: 
937:     removePieceFromSquare(selectedSquare); // Remove sprite from old square
938:     deselectPiece(pieceToMove, squareClicked); // Add sprite to new square and deselect piece
939:     chessScene->update();
940: 
941:     // Reset all move variables
942:     resetPossibleMoveSquares();
943:     resetHighlightedSquares();
944:     selectedSquare->resetColor();
945:     selectedSquare = nullptr;
946:     movePending = false;
947: 
948:     if (pieceToMove->getName() == "Pawn") {
949:         // Pawn specific (en passant)
950:         Pawn* pawn = dynamic_cast<Pawn*>(pieceToMove);
951:         pawn->incrementMoveCounter();
952:     } else if (pieceToMove->getName() == "Rook") {
953:         // Rook specific (castling)
954:         Rook *rook = dynamic_cast<Rook*>(pieceToMove);
955:         if (rook->moved == false) {
956:             rook->moved = true;
957:         }
958:     } else if (pieceToMove->getName() == "King") {
959:         // King specific (castling/check)
960:         King *king = dynamic_cast<King*>(pieceToMove);
961:         if (king->moved == false) {
962:             king->moved = true;
963:         }
964:         king->rank = squareClicked->getRank();
965:         king->file = squareClicked->getFile();
966:     }
967: 
968:     // If en passant capture, remove captured pawn
969:     if (squareClicked == enPassantSquare) {
970:         int rank = enPassantPiece->getWhite() == true ? enPassantSquare->getRank() - 1 : enPassantSquare->getRank() + 1;
971:         removePieceFromSquare(boardSquares[rank][enPassantSquare->getFile()]);
972:     }
973: 
974:     // Update game counter
975:     if (pieceToMove->getWhite() == true) {
976:         halfMoveCounter ++;
977:     } else {
978:         fullMoveCounter += 2;
979:     }
980: 
981:     whiteToPlay = whiteToPlay == true ? false : true;
982:     lastMovedPiece = pieceToMove;
983:     manageEnPassant();
984: 
985:      // getStats();
986: 
987:     return;
988: }
989: 
990: void ChessBoard::moveBlack()
991: {
992:     qDebug() << "----------------------------------------------------------------";
993:     qDebug() << "Black moving...";
994: 
995:     //    Q_EMIT switchMascot(1);
996:     // Randomly sleep to simulate thinking of computer
997:     QElapsedTimer timer;
998:     timer.start();
999: 
1000:     std::random_device random_gen;
1001:     std::mt19937 gen(random_gen());
1002:     std::uniform_int_distribution<int> distribution(2, 5);
1003:     int random_number = distribution(gen);
1004:     while (timer.elapsed() < random_number * 1000) {
1005: 
1006:     }
1007: 
1008:     selectedSquare = nextBestMoveSquares[1];
1009:     this->movePiece(nextBestMoveSquares[0]);
1010:     selectedSquare = nullptr;
1011: 
1012:     whiteToPlay = true;
1013: 
1014:      // getStats();
1015:     //    Q_EMIT switchMascot(0);
1016:     Q_EMIT moveCompleted(lastMove, eval.winning, eval.value);
1017: 
1018:     return;
1019: }

1021: // This function is responsible for:
1022: // - updating the pieces "selected" flag
1023: // - changing the color of the piece on the board to the selected color
1024: void ChessBoard::selectPiece(ChessPiece *selectedPiece, ChessSquare *square) {
1025:     selectedPiece->setIsSelected(true);
1026: 
1027:     // Remove and add piece to change sprite color (can probably be done better)
1028:     removePieceFromSquare(square);
1029:     addPieceToSquare(selectedPiece, square->getRank(), square->getFile(), 3);
1030: 
1031:     return;
1032: }
1033: 
1034: /* This function is responsible for:
1035:  * - literally moving the piece
1036:  * - updating the pieces "selected" flag
1037:  * - changing the color of the piece on the board back to its base color
1038:  */
1039: void ChessBoard::deselectPiece(ChessPiece *selectedPiece, ChessSquare *square) {
1040:     selectedPiece->setIsSelected(false);
1041:     int pieceBaseColor = selectedPiece->getWhite() == true ? 1 : 2;
1042:     removePieceFromSquare(square);
1043:     addPieceToSquare(selectedPiece, square->getRank(), square->getFile(), pieceBaseColor);
1044: 
1045:     return;
1046: }
1047: 
1048: /* This function is responsible for:
1049:  * - creating a sprite of the piece in the appropriate size and color
1050:  *   [Color code: 1 - white, 2 - black, 3 - selected]
1051:  * - placing it centered on the correct square
1052:  * - update the occupyingpiece pointer of said square
1053:  * - update the sprite pointer for the piece
1054:  */
1055: void ChessBoard::addPieceToSquare(ChessPiece *piece, int rank, int file, int color)
1056: {
1057:     // These values are set based on cosmetic appearance
1058:     int offsetX = 5, offsetY = 5, shrinkX = 10, shrinkY = 10;
1059: 
1060:     // Create and scale the sprite
1061:     QPixmap pieceSprite;
1062:     if (color == 2) { pieceSprite = piece->getDarkIcon(); }
1063:     else if (color == 1) { pieceSprite = piece->getLightIcon(); }
1064:     else if (color == 3) { pieceSprite = piece->getSelectedIcon(); }
1065:     ChessSquare *squares = boardSquares[rank][file];
1066:     QPixmap scaledPiece = pieceSprite.scaled(tileSize-shrinkX, tileSize-shrinkY, Qt::KeepAspectRatio);
1067:     QGraphicsPixmapItem *finalSprite = new QGraphicsPixmapItem(scaledPiece);
1068: 
1069:     // Position and add to scene
1070:     finalSprite->setPos(squares->rect().topLeft() + QPointF(offsetX, offsetY));
1071:     chessScene->addItem(finalSprite);
1072: 
1073:     // Add to associated ChessSquare object
1074:     ChessSquare *square = boardSquares[rank][file];
1075:     square->setOccupyingPiece(piece);
1076:     piece->setSprite(finalSprite);
1077: 
1078:     return;
1079: }
1080: 
1081: // This function is responsible for:
1082: // - remove the sprite from the square
1083: // - set the occupyingpiece pointer of square to nullptr
1084: void ChessBoard::removePieceFromSquare(ChessSquare *square)
1085: {
1086:     ChessPiece *piece = square->getOccupyingPiece();
1087:     if (piece == nullptr) {
1088:         // qDebug() << "Attempting to remove nullptr from square -- aborting.";
1089:         return;
1090:     } else {
1091:         QGraphicsPixmapItem *sprite = piece->getSprite();
1092:         if (sprite) {
1093:             // qDebug() << "Removing sprite from square.";
1094:             chessScene->removeItem(sprite);
1095:         } else {
1096:             // qDebug() << "Sprite pointer is null.";
1097:         }
1098:         square->setOccupyingPiece(nullptr);
1099:     }
1100: 
1101:     return;
1102: }
1103: 
1104: // ----------------------------------------- //
1105: // CHESS STATUS RELATED FUNCTIONS //
1106: // ---------------------------------------- //
1107: 
1108: // This function checks en passant status by:
1109: // -
1110: //
1111: // Restrictions: only detects one en passant square at a time
1112: // Note: this function utilizes normal chess rank and file numberings
1113: void ChessBoard::manageEnPassant()
1114: {
1115:     QColor color = QColor(241,235,156);
1116:     if (enPassantSquare != nullptr) { enPassantCounter ++; }
1117: 
1118:     // Reset en passant status if expired
1119:     if (enPassantCounter > 1) {
1120:         enPassantCounter = 0;
1121:         enPassantPiece = nullptr;
1122:         enPassantSquare->resetColor();
1123:         enPassantSquare = nullptr;
1124:     }
1125: 
1126:     // If a pawn moved last
1127:     if (lastMovedPiece->getName() == "Pawn") {
1128:         Pawn* pawn = dynamic_cast<Pawn*>(lastMovedPiece);
1129:         std::string lastMoveString = lastMove.toStdString();
1130:         qDebug() << "Last move string:" << lastMoveString;
1131: 
1132:         // If it was the pawns first move, get the rank the pawn is on from the last move (algebraic notation)
1133:         if (pawn->getMoveCounter() == 1) {
1134:             std::string rankString = lastMoveString.substr(lastMoveString.size()-1, 1);
1135:             int vulnerableRank;
1136:             std::stringstream(rankString) >> vulnerableRank;
1137:             qDebug() << "Vulnerable rank:" << vulnerableRank;
1138: 
1139:             // If it was a two-space move
1140:             if (vulnerableRank == 4 || vulnerableRank == 5) {
1141:                 if(vulnerableRank == 5) { vulnerableRank = 3; }
1142: 
1143:                 // Determine the possible attacking files (the files to the left and right of the pawn)
1144:                 int rightAttackFile = static_cast<int>(lastMoveString.substr(lastMoveString.size()-2, 1)[0]) - 96;
1145:                 int leftAttackFile = static_cast<int>(lastMoveString.substr(lastMoveString.size()-2, 1)[0]) - 98;
1146:                 qDebug() << "Left attack file:" << leftAttackFile << " Right attack file:" << rightAttackFile;
1147: 
1148:                 // If the left attack file is on the board and occupied by an opposing pawn
1149:                 if (leftAttackFile >= 0) {
1150:                     ChessPiece *attackingPiece = boardSquares[vulnerableRank][leftAttackFile]->getOccupyingPiece();
1151:                     if (attackingPiece != nullptr && attackingPiece->getName() == "Pawn" && attackingPiece->getWhite() != pawn->getWhite()) {
1152:                         // Target rank depends on piece color
1153:                         if (pawn->getWhite() == true) {
1154:                             vulnerableRank = vulnerableRank + 1;
1155:                         } else {
1156:                             vulnerableRank = vulnerableRank - 1;
1157:                         }
1158:                         enPassantSquare = boardSquares[vulnerableRank][leftAttackFile + 1];
1159:                         if (config->getAssistModeOn() == true) { enPassantSquare->toggleSquareCustom(color); }
1160:                         enPassantPiece = pawn;
1161:                         qDebug() << "en passant square:" << enPassantSquare->getRank() << enPassantSquare->getFile();
1162:                         return;
1163:                     }
1164:                 }
1165:                 // If the right attack file is on the board and occupied by an opposing pawn
1166:                 if (rightAttackFile <= 7) {
1167:                     ChessPiece *attackingPiece = boardSquares[vulnerableRank][rightAttackFile]->getOccupyingPiece();
1168:                     if (attackingPiece != nullptr && attackingPiece->getName() == "Pawn" && attackingPiece->getWhite() != pawn->getWhite()) {
1169:                         // Target rank depends on piece color
1170:                         if (pawn->getWhite() == true) {
1171:                             vulnerableRank = vulnerableRank + 1;
1172:                         } else {
1173:                             vulnerableRank = vulnerableRank - 1;
1174:                         }
1175:                         enPassantSquare = boardSquares[vulnerableRank][rightAttackFile - 1];
1176:                         if (config->getAssistModeOn() == true) { enPassantSquare->toggleSquareCustom(color); }
1177:                         enPassantPiece = pawn;
1178:                         qDebug() << "en passant square:" << enPassantSquare->getRank() << enPassantSquare->getFile();
1179:                         return;
1180:                     }
1181:                 }
1182:             }
1183:         }
1184:     }
1185:     return;
1186: }
1187: 
1188: QString ChessBoard::getCastlingRights()
1189: {
1190:     // Can update this function with global BQCastle, BKCastle, WKCastle, WQCastle variables to skip iterating through each time
1191:     // once castling is lost, since it is never regained.
1192:     QString uci;
1193:     bool castling = false;
1194: 
1195:     if (whiteKing->moved == false) {
1196:         if (whiteKingsideRook != nullptr && whiteKingsideRook->moved == false) {
1197:             uci = uci + "K";
1198:             castling = true;
1199:             if (boardSquares[7][1]->getOccupyingPiece() == nullptr && boardSquares[7][2]->getOccupyingPiece() == nullptr) {
1200:                 // Logic for adding to possible squares
1201:             }
1202:         }
1203:         if (whiteQueensideRook != nullptr && whiteQueensideRook->moved == false) {
1204:             uci = uci + "Q";
1205:             castling = true;
1206:             if (boardSquares[7][4]->getOccupyingPiece() == nullptr && boardSquares[7][5]->getOccupyingPiece() == nullptr && boardSquares[7][6]->getOccupyingPiece() == nullptr) {
1207:                 // Logic for adding to possible squares
1208:             }
1209:         }
1210:     }
1211:     if (blackKing -> moved == false) {
1212:         if (blackKingsideRook != nullptr && blackKingsideRook->moved == false) {
1213:             uci = uci + "k";
1214:             castling = true;
1215:             if (boardSquares[0][1]->getOccupyingPiece() == nullptr && boardSquares[0][2]->getOccupyingPiece() == nullptr) {
1216:                 // Logic for adding to possible squares
1217:             }
1218:         }
1219:         if (blackQueensideRook != nullptr && blackQueensideRook->moved == false) {
1220:             uci = uci + "q";
1221:             castling = true;
1222:             if (boardSquares[0][4]->getOccupyingPiece() == nullptr && boardSquares[0][5]->getOccupyingPiece() == nullptr && boardSquares[0][6]->getOccupyingPiece() == nullptr) {
1223:                 // Logic for adding to possible squares
1224:             }
1225:         }
1226:     }
1227: 
1228:     if (castling == false) {
1229:         uci = uci + "-";
1230:     }
1231: 
1232:     return uci;
1233: }
1234: 
1235: // ------------------------------------- //
1236: // NOTATION RELATED FUNCTIONS //
1237: // ------------------------------------- //
1238: 
1239: QString ChessBoard::boardToUCI()
1240: {
1241:     QString uci;
1242: 
1243:     for (int i = 0; i < 8; i++) {
1244:         // New rank
1245:         int emptySquares = 0;
1246: 
1247:         for (int j = 0; j < 8; j++) {
1248:             // For each file on that rank
1249:             // If that square has a piece
1250:             if (boardSquares[i][j]->getOccupyingPiece() != nullptr) {
1251:                 // Decide whether to precede with ".", number, or nothing
1252:                 if (emptySquares >= 1) {
1253:                     uci = uci + QString::fromStdString(std::to_string(emptySquares));
1254:                 }
1255:                 uci = uci + boardSquares[i][j]->getOccupyingPiece()->getFEN();
1256:                 emptySquares = 0;
1257:             } else {
1258:                 emptySquares ++;
1259:             }
1260:         }
1261:         // Need to account for trailing empty squares
1262:         if (emptySquares >= 1) {
1263:             uci = uci + QString::fromStdString(std::to_string(emptySquares));
1264:         }
1265:         // End rank
1266:         if (i < 7) {
1267:             uci = uci + "/";
1268:         }
1269:     }
1270:     // Denote whose turn it is
1271:     uci = uci + " ";
1272:     uci = whiteToPlay ? uci + "w" : uci + "b";
1273:     // Denote castling rights
1274:     uci = uci + " ";
1275:     uci = uci + this->getCastlingRights();
1276:     // Denote en passant status
1277:     uci = uci + " ";
1278:     if (enPassantSquare != nullptr) {
1279:         ChessPiece *pawn = new ChessPiece(this->config->getColor());
1280:         uci = uci + this->moveToAlgebraic(pawn, enPassantSquare);
1281:     } else {
1282:         uci = uci + "-";
1283:     }
1284:     // Denote halfmove and fullmove
1285:     uci = uci + " ";
1286:     uci = uci + QString::fromStdString(std::to_string(halfMoveCounter));
1287:     uci = uci + " ";
1288:     uci = uci + QString::fromStdString(std::to_string(fullMoveCounter));
1289: 
1290:     qDebug() << uci;
1291: 
1292:     return uci;
1293: }
1294: 
1295: /* Convert the most recent move into algebraic notation */
1296: QString ChessBoard::moveToAlgebraic(ChessPiece *movedPiece, ChessSquare *square)
1297: {
1298:     QString piece, algebraic;
1299:     QString name = movedPiece->getName();
1300: 
1301:     if (name == "Pawn") {
1302:         // pawns dont get letter appended
1303:     } else if (name == "Rook") {
1304:         piece = piece + "R";
1305:     } else if (name == "Knight") {
1306:         piece = piece + "N";
1307:     } else if (name == "Bishop") {
1308:         piece = piece + "B";
1309:     } else if (name == "Queen") {
1310:         piece = piece + "Q";
1311:     } else if (name == "King") {
1312:         piece = piece + "K";
1313:     } else {
1314:         qDebug() << "Error getting piece type in moveToAlgebraic()";
1315:     }
1316: 
1317:     char file = 96 + square->getFile() + 1;
1318:     int rank = 8 - square->getRank();
1319: 
1320:     if (square->getOccupyingPiece() != nullptr) {
1321:         algebraic = piece + "x" + file + QString::fromStdString(std::to_string(rank));
1322:     } else {
1323:         algebraic = piece + file + QString::fromStdString(std::to_string(rank));
1324:     }
1325: 
1326:     return algebraic;
1327: }

102:         int value = 0; // Represents advantage if cp, or moves until mate if mate
103:         int winning = 0;  // 1 - white, 2 - black
104:         int status = 0;   // 1 - cp, 2 - mate
105:     };

17: QPixmap ChessPiece::getIcon() {
18:     return icon;
19: }
20: 
21: QPixmap ChessPiece::getLightIcon()
22: {
23:     QPixmap originalDarkIcon = this->getIcon();
24:     QPixmap lightIcon = originalDarkIcon.scaled(originalDarkIcon.size());
25:     QPainter painter(&lightIcon);
26:     QColor color = QColor(255, 255, 255);
27: 
28:     painter.setCompositionMode(QPainter::CompositionMode_Source);
29:     painter.fillRect(lightIcon.rect(), color);
30:     painter.setCompositionMode(QPainter::CompositionMode_DestinationIn);
31:     painter.drawPixmap(0, 0, originalDarkIcon);
32:     painter.end();
33: 
34:     return lightIcon;
35: 
36: }
37: 
38: QPixmap ChessPiece::getDarkIcon()
39: {
40:     return this->getIcon();
41: 
42: }
43: 
44: QPixmap ChessPiece::getPlayerIcon()
45: {
46:     if (this->playerIsWhite == true) {
47:         return this->getLightIcon();
48:     } else {
49:         return this->getDarkIcon();
50:     }
51: }
52: 
53: QPixmap ChessPiece::getOppIcon()
54: {
55:     if (this->playerIsWhite == false) {
56:         return this->getLightIcon();
57:     } else {
58:         return this->getDarkIcon();
59:     }
60: }
61: 
62: QPixmap ChessPiece::getSelectedIcon()
63: {
64:     QPixmap originalDarkIcon = this->getIcon();
65:     QPixmap lightIcon = originalDarkIcon.scaled(originalDarkIcon.size());
66:     QPainter painter(&lightIcon);
67:     QColor color;
68:     if (this->getWhite() == true) {
69:         color.setRgb(96,129,153);
70:     } else {
71:         color.setRgb(96,129,153);
72:     }
73: 
74:     painter.setCompositionMode(QPainter::CompositionMode_Source);
75:     painter.fillRect(lightIcon.rect(), color);
76:     painter.setCompositionMode(QPainter::CompositionMode_DestinationIn);
77:     painter.drawPixmap(0, 0, originalDarkIcon);
78:     painter.end();
79: 
80:     return lightIcon;
81: }
82: 
83: QString ChessPiece::getFEN()
84: {
85:     if (this->name == "Pawn") {
86:         if (this -> color == 1) {
87:             return "P";
88:         } else {
89:             return "p";
90:         }
91:     } else if (this->name == "Rook") {
92:         if (this -> color == 1) {
93:             return "R";
94:         } else {
95:             return "r";
96:         }
97:     } else if (this->name == "Knight") {
98:         if (this -> color == 1) {
99:             return "N";
100:         } else {
101:             return "n";
102:         }
103:     } else if (this->name == "Bishop") {
104:         if (this -> color == 1) {
105:             return "B";
106:         } else {
107:             return "b";
108:         }
109:     } else if (this->name == "Queen") {
110:         if (this -> color == 1) {
111:             return "Q";
112:         } else {
113:             return "q";
114:         }
115:     } else if (this->name == "King") {
116:         if (this -> color == 1) {
117:             return "K";
118:         } else {
119:             return "k";
120:         }
121:     } else {
122:         return "FEN ERROR";
123:     }
124: }

181:     }

11: ChessSquare::ChessSquare(int posX, int posY, int width, int height, bool white)
12:     : QGraphicsRectItem(posX, posY, width, height)
13: {
14:     this->playerIsWhite = white;
15:     this->rank = posX;
16:     this->file = posY;
17:     setBaseColor(posX, posY);
18: }
19: 
20: void ChessSquare::setBaseColor(int rank, int file) {
21: 
22:     QColor baseColor = this->getBaseColor();
23: 
24:     if ((rank + file) % 2 != 0) {
25:         this->setBrush(baseColor);
26:     } else {
27:         this->setBrush(baseColor);
28:     }
29:     return;
30: }
31: 
32: QColor ChessSquare::getBaseColor() {
33:     QColor bottomLeftColor;
34:     QColor otherColor;
35: 
36:     bottomLeftColor = QColor(206,212,218);
37:     otherColor = QColor(52,58,64);
38: 
39:     if ((rank + file) % 2 != 0) {
40:         return otherColor;
41:     } else {
42:         return bottomLeftColor;
43:     }
44: }
45: 
46: void ChessSquare::mousePressEvent(QGraphicsSceneMouseEvent *event)
47: {
48:     if (disabled == true) {
49:         event->ignore();
50:     } else {
51:         if (event->button() == Qt::RightButton) {           // Right mouse click event
52:             rightClick();
53:         } else if (event->button() == Qt::LeftButton) {     // Left mouse click event
54:             leftClick();
55:         }
56:     }
57:     return;
58: }
59: 
60: // On left "main" click
61: void ChessSquare::leftClick()
62: {
63:     Q_EMIT squareLeftClicked(rank, file);
64:     return;
65: }
66: 
67: // On right click
68: void ChessSquare::rightClick()
69: {
70:     Q_EMIT squareRightClicked(rank, file);
71:     return;
72: }
73: 
74: void ChessSquare::toggleSquareRed() {
75:     if (!(this->brush().color() == QColor(129, 65, 65))) {
76:         this->setBrush(QColor(129, 65, 65));
77:     } else {
78:         setBaseColor(rank, file);
79:     }
80:     return;
81: }
82: 
83: void ChessSquare::toggleSquareYellow() {
84:     // Check to see if it is already yellow
85:     if (this->brush().color() == this->getBaseColor()) {
86:         QColor whiteColor = QColor(206,212,218);
87:         if (this->getBaseColor() == whiteColor) {
88:             // Light sqaures
89:             this->setBrush(QColor(255,240,173));
90:         } else {
91:             // Dark squares
92:             this->setBrush(QColor(252,226,108));
93:         }
94:     } else {
95:         setBaseColor(rank, file);
96:     }
97:     return;
98: }
99: 
100: void ChessSquare::resetColor()
101: {
102:     setBaseColor(rank, file);
103:     return;
104: }
105: 
106: void ChessSquare::toggleSquareCustom(QColor color)
107: {
108:     this->setBrush(color);
109:     return;
110: }
111:

115: {
116:     return occupyingPiece;
117: }
118: 
119: void ChessSquare::setOccupyingPiece(ChessPiece *newOccupyingPiece)
120: {
121:     occupyingPiece = newOccupyingPiece;
122:     return;
123: }

128:         this->rank = rank;
129:     }
130:     return;
131: }

134: {
135:     if (file >= 0 && file < 8) {
136:         this->file = file;
137:     }
138:     return;
139: }

142: {

144: }

19: {

22:

24:     db.setPort(5432);

26:     db.setUserName("postgres");

35:      */
36: 
37:     return 1;

39: 
40: int Config::parseJSON() {
41:     QFile m_configFile(m_configPath);
42: 
43:     // Check for file open error
44:     if (!m_configFile.open(QIODevice::ReadOnly)) {
45:         qDebug() << "Failed to open JSON file:" << m_configFile.errorString();
46:         return 0;
47:     }
48: 
49:     QByteArray jsonData = m_configFile.readAll();
50:     m_configFile.close();
51: 
52:     QJsonParseError parseError;
53:     QJsonDocument doc = QJsonDocument::fromJson(jsonData, &parseError);
54:     // Check for json parsing error
55:     if (doc.isNull()) {
56:         qDebug() << "Failed to parse JSON:" << parseError.errorString();
57:         return 0;
58:     }
59: 
60:     // Check for object error
61:     if (!doc.isObject()) {
62:         qDebug() << "JSON document is not an object";
63:         return 0;
64:     }
65: 
66:     m_rootObject = doc.object();
67: 
68:     return 1;
69: }
70: 
71: void Config::refreshConfig()
72: {
73:     // Set up the database connection
74:     Config dbConfig;
75:     dbConfig.openDatabase();
76: 
77:     // Execute a query to select all attributes from the table "configuration"
78:     QString queryString = "SELECT config_color, config_assist, config_difficulty FROM configuration WHERE config_id = 1";
79:     QSqlQuery query;
80:     query.prepare(queryString);
81:     if (!query.exec()) {
82:         qWarning() << "Error: Unable to execute query:" << query.lastError().text();
83:     } else {
84:         if (query.next()) { // Check if there is at least one record
85:             bool configColor = query.value(0).toBool();
86:             bool configAssist = query.value(1).toBool();
87:             int configDifficulty = query.value(2).toInt();
88:             this->setAssistModeOn(configAssist);
89:             this->setDifficulty(configDifficulty);
90:             this->setColor(configColor);
91:             qDebug() << "Updating config object, setting assist to:" << configAssist << "and color to:" << configColor << "and diff to:" << configDifficulty;
92:         } else {
93:             qWarning() << "No configuration found for config_id = 1";
94:         }
95:     }
96: 
97:     query.clear();
98:     dbConfig.closeDatabase();
99:     return;
100: }
101: 
102: void Config::saveConfig()
103: {
104:     Config dbConfig;
105:     dbConfig.openDatabase();
106: 
107:         QString insertQuery = "UPDATE configuration SET config_color = ?, config_assist = ?, config_difficulty = ? WHERE config_id = 1";
108:         QSqlQuery query;
109:         query.prepare(insertQuery);
110:         query.addBindValue(this->color);
111:         query.addBindValue(this->assistModeOn);
112:         query.addBindValue(this->difficulty);
113: 
114:         if (!query.exec()) {
115:             qDebug() << "Error executing update query:" << query.lastError().text();
116:             return ;
117:         }
118: 
119:     query.clear();
120:     dbConfig.closeDatabase();
121:     return;
122: }
123: 
124: int Config::getDifficulty() const
125: {
126:     return difficulty;
127: }
128: 
129: void Config::setDifficulty(int newDifficulty)
130: {
131:     difficulty = newDifficulty;
132: }
133: 
134: bool Config::getColor() const
135: {
136:     return color;
137: }
138: 
139: void Config::setColor(bool newColor)
140: {
141:     color = newColor;
142: }
143: 
144: bool Config::getAssistModeOn() const
145: {
146:     return assistModeOn;
147: }
148: 
149: void Config::setAssistModeOn(bool newAssistModeOn)
150: {
151:     assistModeOn = newAssistModeOn;
152: }
153: 
154: int Config::openDatabase()
155: {
156:     bool connectioncheck = db.open();
157: 
158:     if (connectioncheck == true){
159:         // qDebug() << "Connection to database established." << Qt::endl;
160:         return 1;
161:     } else {
162:         qDebug() << QSqlDatabase::drivers() << Qt::endl;
163:         qDebug() << "Error opening database " << db.databaseName() << " :" << db.lastError().text() << Qt::endl;
164:         return 0;
165:     }
166: }
167: 
168: int Config::closeDatabase()
169: {
170:     if (db.isOpen()) {
171:         db.close();
172:         // qDebug() << "Database closed.";
173:         return 1;
174:     } else {
175:         qDebug() << "No database open.";
176:         return 0;
177:     }
178: }
